⏺ Audit breakdown — six specialists

  Per-agent gist (one line each):

  - architect-reviewer: Filter+pagination over annotated queryset is unverified;
   make test skips unit tests; updated_at won't fire without explicit save.
  - postgres-pro: Filter-by-status is O(N) at scale — recommends partial indexes
   or denormalization; verify EXPLAIN at 1M rows not 10k; lock connection
  pooling.
  - devops-engineer: Pin Playwright tag; bump backend healthcheck timing; logs
  bind-mount fragile on cold clone; .env preflight needed.
  - qa-expert: No DB-reset between Playwright runs; one-spec-multi-block creates
   ordering coupling; pytest-django + transaction=True + async needs an explicit
   fixture pattern.
  - adsk:security-engineer: DJANGO_DEBUG=False not set explicitly; validation
  logger.exception leaks user input; Playwright runs as root by default.
  - api-designer: Add Location header on POST 201; expose OpenAPI docs; clarify
  ordering is opaque-passthrough on FE.

  Cross-cutting fixes now baked into the plan:

     │                                                                         │
     │ - PATCH semantics: spec says PATCH "involves creating a new JobStatus   │
     │ entry." Read literally, name is set on POST and not mutable through     │
     │ PATCH. Lock: PATCH only accepts status_type. Name is immutable          │
     │ post-creation. (Open question for user.) PATCH-as-append is mildly      │
     │ non-RESTful (POST /api/jobs/<id>/statuses/ would be the purer verb),    │
     │ but we follow the spec wording literally and document the tradeoff in   │
     │ README.                                                                 │
     │ - Status set: spec says "at least four distinct states" with PENDING /  │
     │ RUNNING / COMPLETED / FAILED as examples. Lock the four exact values;   │
     │ no CANCELLED.                                                           │
     │ - current_status when no JobStatus exists: theoretically impossible     │
     │ because POST creates initial PENDING. Defensive: serializer returns     │
     │ null if no rows, but never expected in practice.                        │

     │ │ id          │ bigint      │ PK, auto            │                     │
     │    │                                                                    │
     │ ├─────────────┼─────────────┼─────────────────────┼──────────────────── │
     │ ───┤                                                                    │
     │ │             │             │ NOT NULL, FK →      │ Indexed via         │
     │ composite │                                                             │
     │ │ job_id      │ bigint      │ jobs_job(id),       │  below              │
     │    │                                                                    │
     │ │             │             │ on_delete=CASCADE   │                     │
     │    │                                                                    │
     │ ├─────────────┼─────────────┼─────────────────────┼──────────────────── │
     │ ───┤                                                                    │
     │ │             │             │ NOT NULL,           │ Django TextChoices  │
     │    │                                                                    │
     │ │ status_type │ varchar(16) │ choices-checked at  │ enum {PENDING,      │
     │    │                                                                    │
     │ │             │             │ app layer           │ RUNNING, COMPLETED, │
     │    │                                                                    │
     │ │             │             │                     │ FAILED}             │
     │    │                                                                    │
     │ ├─────────────┼─────────────┼─────────────────────┼──────────────────── │
     │ ───┤                                                                    │
     │ │ timestamp   │ timestamptz │ NOT NULL, default   │ Django              │
     │    │                                                                    │
     │ │             │             │ now()               │ auto_now_add=True   │
     │    │                                                                    │
     │ └─────────────┴─────────────┴─────────────────────┴──────────────────── │
     │ ───┘                                                                    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Indexes                                                                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ index: jobs_job_pkey                                                    │
     │ columns: (id)                                                           │
     │ rationale: PK, default                                                  │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ index: jobs_jobstatus_pkey                                              │
     │ columns: (id)                                                           │
     │ rationale: PK, default                                                  │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ index: idx_jobstatus_job_timestamp_desc                                 │
     │ columns: (job_id, timestamp DESC)                                       │
     │ rationale: Hot path: latest-status lookup per job (Subquery+OuterRef in │
     │  list                                                                   │
     │   endpoint) and history endpoint ordering. Single composite serves      │
     │ both.                                                                   │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ index: idx_job_created_at_id_desc                                       │
     │ columns: (created_at DESC, id DESC)                                     │
     │ rationale: Default cursor pagination on list endpoint. Composite        │
     │ ensures                                                                 │
     │   stability under inserts. Verify utility via EXPLAIN; Postgres can     │
     │ sometimes                                                               │
     │   scan PK index backwards for similar effect.                           │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ index: Per-status partial indexes (TBD)                                 │
     │ columns: (job_id, timestamp DESC) WHERE status_type='X'                 │
     │ rationale: Considered for filter-by-status performance; locked at       │
     │ /spec:design.                                                           │
     │   See section 8.                                                        │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ index: idx_job_name                                                     │
     │ columns: (name)                                                         │
     │ rationale: Optional. Add only if benchmarking shows name filter/sort is │
     │  hot.                                                                   │
     │   Default: skip.                                                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ name does not need uniqueness — spec doesn't require it, and the same   │
     │ job name can legitimately recur.                                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Constraints and invariants                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Every Job always has at least one JobStatus (enforced transactionally │
     │  by the create service: Job insert + JobStatus(PENDING) insert in one   │
     │ atomic block). No DB constraint expresses this — it would be a          │
     │ chicken-and-egg with the FK.                                            │
     │ - status_type is constrained at the application layer by Django's       │
     │ TextChoices and Pydantic's Enum. DB-level CHECK constraint is a         │
     │ single-line Meta.constraints =                                          │
     │ [CheckConstraint(check=Q(status_type__in=StatusType.values),            │
     │ name="jobstatus_status_type_valid")]; defer unless the DB-integrity     │
     │ reviewer concern surfaces. (Open question.)                             │
     │ - Cascade delete on the FK ensures DELETE /api/jobs/<id>/ removes all   │
     │ related JobStatus rows.                                                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Sharding / partitioning                                                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ For the millions-of-jobs scenario on a single Postgres instance, no     │
     │ sharding or partitioning is needed at this scope. Postgres handles low  │
     │ billions of rows on commodity hardware with the indexes above.          │
     │ Rationale documented in CLAUDE.md so future contributors don't add      │
     │ premature complexity.                                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ If the project ever crossed thresholds:                                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - jobs_jobstatus is the bigger table (one row per status change per     │
     │ job). At ~100M+ rows: range-partition by timestamp monthly. The         │
     │ composite (job_id, timestamp DESC) index continues to work per          │
     │ partition.                                                              │
     │ - jobs_job is unlikely to ever need partitioning.                       │
     │ - No application-level sharding considered. Multi-tenancy → partition   │
     │ or shard by tenant_id. Not in scope.                                    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ 5. Locked API contract                                                  │
     │                                                                         │
     │ JSON path prefix is /api. All timestamps are ISO 8601 UTC with Z. All   │
     │ cursors are opaque base64 strings.                                      │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Cross-cutting:                                                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - OpenAPI schema is served at /api/openapi.json and interactive docs at │
     │  /api/docs/ (Ninja auto-generates) — exposed in all environments for    │
     │ evaluator convenience.                                                  │
     │ - No /v1/ prefix; versioning deferred — no external consumers in scope. │
     │ - ordering is treated as an opaque string passthrough on the FE (no     │
     │ client-side decomposition into field+direction); this pins the TanStack │
     │  Query key shape.                                                       │
     │ - Same-origin (FE serves /api/* via nginx proxy) means CORS is a        │
     │ non-issue.                                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Error envelope (used everywhere)                                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ {                                                                       │
     │   "detail": "Validation failed",                                        │
     │   "errors": [                                                           │
     │     { "loc": ["body", "name"], "msg": "Name cannot be empty", "type":   │
     │ "value_error" }                                                         │
     │   ]                                                                     │
     │ }                                                                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ errors omitted on non-validation errors (e.g. 404). Status codes: 400   │
     │ validation, 404 not found, 500 server error.                            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ GET /api/jobs/                                                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Query params (all optional):                                            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - status — one of PENDING|RUNNING|COMPLETED|FAILED. Filters by current  │
     │ status.                                                                 │
     │ - ordering — one of name|-name|created_at|-created_at. Default          │
     │ -created_at.                                                            │
     │ - cursor — opaque cursor from a previous response.                      │
     │ - limit — page size, default 20, max 100.                               │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Response 200:                                                           │
     │                                                                         │
     │ {                                                                       │
     │   "results": [                                                          │
     │     {                                                                   │
     │       "id": 1,                                                          │
     │       "name": "Fluid Dynamics Simulation",                              │
     │       "current_status": "PENDING",                                      │
     │       "created_at": "2026-04-25T10:00:00Z",                             │
     │       "updated_at": "2026-04-25T10:00:00Z"                              │
     │     }                                                                   │
     │   ],                                                                    │
     │   "next":                                                               │
     │ "eyJjcmVhdGVkX2F0IjoiMjAyNi0wNC0yNVQxMDowMDowMFoiLCJpZCI6MX0=",         │
     │   "previous": null                                                      │
     │ }                                                                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ POST /api/jobs/                                                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Request:                                                                │
     │                                                                         │
     │ { "name": "Fluid Dynamics Simulation" }                                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Validation: name non-empty, max 200 chars.                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Response 201, with header Location: /api/jobs/<id>/:                    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ {                                                                       │
     │   "id": 1,                                                              │
     │   "name": "Fluid Dynamics Simulation",                                  │
     │   "current_status": "PENDING",                                          │
     │   "created_at": "2026-04-25T10:00:00Z",                                 │
     │   "updated_at": "2026-04-25T10:00:00Z"                                  │
     │ }                                                                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Side effect: JobStatus(job=job, status_type=PENDING) row created in the │
     │  same transaction.                                                      │
     │                                                                         │
     │ GET /api/jobs/<id>/                                                     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Response 200: same shape as the POST response. 404 envelope if not      │
     │ found.                                                                  │
     │                                                                         │
     │ PATCH /api/jobs/<id>/                                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Request:                                                                │
     │                                                                         │
     │ { "status_type": "RUNNING" }                                            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Validation: status_type must be one of the four values. Body must       │
     │ contain only status_type (extra fields rejected).                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Response 200: same shape as detail response, with the new               │
     │ current_status and bumped updated_at.                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Side effect: appends a new JobStatus(job=job, status_type=...) row AND  │
     │ explicitly calls job.save(update_fields=["updated_at"]) to fire         │
     │ auto_now. Both happen in the same atomic block.                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ DELETE /api/jobs/<id>/                                                  │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Response 204, no body. Cascade-deletes JobStatus rows via FK            │
     │ on_delete=CASCADE.                                                      │
     │                                                                         │
     │ GET /api/jobs/<id>/statuses/                                            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Query params: cursor, limit (same as list endpoint). Ordering is fixed  │
     │ -timestamp.                                                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Response 200:                                                           │
     │                                                                         │
     │ {                                                                       │
     │   "results": [                                                          │
     │     { "id": 5, "status_type": "RUNNING", "timestamp":                   │
     │ "2026-04-25T10:30:00Z" },                                               │
     │     { "id": 4, "status_type": "PENDING", "timestamp":                   │
     │ "2026-04-25T10:00:00Z" }                                                │
     │   ],                                                                    │
     │   "next": null,                                                         │
     │   "previous": null                                                      │
     │ }                                                                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Cursor pagination contract                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Use Django Ninja's built-in CursorPagination (shipped stable in         │
     │ v1.6.0). Cursor is base64-encoded (ordering_field, id) tuple. Stable    │
     │ under inserts. Frontend passes next value verbatim back as cursor.      │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Critical at /spec:design: validate that Ninja's CursorPagination works  │
     │ correctly against an annotated, filtered queryset returned from a       │
     │ sync_to_async wrapper. If not, fall back to keyset pagination           │
     │ implemented directly in the service. See section 8 for the underlying   │
     │ perf issue.                                                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ 6. Repo layout                                                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Single monorepo, two service trees plus shared infra at the root.       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ .                                                                       │
     │ ├── README.md                       # front door: prereqs, make         │
     │ targets, contract summary, AI prompts log                               │
     │ ├── Makefile                        # build / up / test / stop / clean  │
     │ ├── docker-compose.yml              # 5 services: db, backend,          │
     │ frontend, vitest (test profile), playwright (test profile)              │
     │ ├── .env.example                    # POSTGRES_*, DJANGO_SECRET_KEY,    │
     │ DJANGO_DEBUG, ENV, LOG_* samples                                        │
     │ ├── .gitignore                      # logs/, *.log, *.log.*, .env,      │
     │ __pycache__, node_modules, dist                                         │
     │ ├── CLAUDE.md                       # project memory; created via       │
     │ `init` at start of phase 2                                              │
     │ ├── backend/                                                            │
     │ │   ├── pyproject.toml              # uv-managed deps                   │
     │ │   ├── uv.lock                                                         │
     │ │   ├── Dockerfile                  # multi-stage with uv; runtime      │
     │ stage installs `curl` for healthcheck                                   │
     │ │   ├── manage.py                                                       │
     │ │   ├── pytest.ini                  # asyncio_mode=auto                 │
     │ │   ├── entrypoint.sh               # waits for db, runs migrate, exec  │
     │ uvicorn (LF line endings, chmod +x)                                     │
     │ │   └── config/                     # Django project package            │
     │ │       ├── __init__.py                                                 │
     │ │       ├── settings.py                                                 │
     │ │       ├── logging.py              # dictConfig factory (text / JSON,  │
     │ color, rotation)                                                        │
     │ │       ├── asgi.py                                                     │
     │ │       ├── urls.py                 # mounts NinjaAPI() at /api         │
     │ │       └── api.py                  # NinjaAPI() instance + jobs router │
     │  include                                                                │
     │ │   └── jobs/                       # the single Django app             │
     │ │       ├── __init__.py                                                 │
     │ │       ├── apps.py                                                     │
     │ │       ├── models.py               # Job, JobStatus, StatusType        │
     │ choices                                                                 │
     │ │       ├── schemas.py              # Pydantic In/Out schemas (Ninja    │
     │ Schema)                                                                 │
     │ │       ├── services.py             # async business logic; all logging │
     │  emits here                                                             │
     │ │       ├── api.py                  # Ninja Router with the six         │
     │ handlers                                                                │
     │ │       ├── migrations/                                                 │
     │ │       └── tests/                                                      │
     │ │           ├── __init__.py                                             │
     │ │           ├── conftest.py         # sync factory fixture,             │
     │ async_client fixture                                                    │
     │ │           ├── factories.py        # factory_boy factories             │
     │ │           ├── test_api.py                                             │
     │ │           └── test_services.py                                        │
     │ ├── frontend/                                                           │
     │ │   ├── package.json                # exact pinned versions;            │
     │ "test:unit": "vitest run"                                               │
     │ │   ├── package-lock.json                                               │
     │ │   ├── tsconfig.json               # strict: true                      │
     │ │   ├── vite.config.ts              # /api proxy, tailwind plugin,      │
     │ test.environment="happy-dom"                                            │
     │ │   ├── tailwind.config.ts                                              │
     │ │   ├── playwright.config.ts        # baseURL via env var; workers: 1;  │
     │ globalSetup for DB reset                                                │
     │ │   ├── eslint.config.js            # flat config                       │
     │ │   ├── .prettierrc                                                     │
     │ │   ├── Dockerfile                  # multi-stage: builder stage (node) │
     │  -> runtime stage (nginx)                                               │
     │ │   ├── Dockerfile.playwright       # FROM                              │
     │ mcr.microsoft.com/playwright:v1.58.2-jammy; USER pwuser                 │
     │ │   ├── nginx.conf                  # try_files for SPA, /api           │
     │ proxy_pass to backend                                                   │
     │ │   ├── index.html                                                      │
     │ │   ├── e2e/                        # per-flow specs for parallelism +  │
     │ isolation                                                               │
     │ │   │   ├── fixtures.ts             # extended `test` with apiReset +   │
     │ seedJob helpers                                                         │
     │ │   │   ├── create.spec.ts                                              │
     │ │   │   ├── update.spec.ts                                              │
     │ │   │   ├── delete.spec.ts                                              │
     │ │   │   └── filter-sort.spec.ts                                         │
     │ │   └── src/                                                            │
     │ │       ├── main.tsx                # mounts router +                   │
     │ QueryClientProvider                                                     │
     │ │       ├── router.tsx              # createBrowserRouter([...])        │
     │ │       ├── setup.ts                # @testing-library/jest-dom         │
     │ matchers                                                                │
     │ │       ├── test-utils/                                                 │
     │ │       │   └── render.tsx          # renderWithProviders (QueryClient  │
     │ + MemoryRouter)                                                         │
     │ │       ├── lib/                                                        │
     │ │       │   ├── api-client.ts       # typed fetch wrapper, error        │
     │ envelope handling                                                       │
     │ │       │   └── query-client.ts     # QueryClient with default options  │
     │ │       ├── components/             # shared primitives (Button,        │
     │ Spinner, Empty, ErrorBanner)                                            │
     │ │       ├── pages/                                                      │
     │ │       │   ├── JobsListPage.tsx                                        │
     │ │       │   └── JobDetailPage.tsx                                       │
     │ │       └── features/jobs/                                              │
     │ │           ├── JobList.tsx         # + JobList.test.tsx                │
     │ │           ├── JobDetail.tsx       # + JobDetail.test.tsx (history     │
     │ rendered inline; no separate JobHistory test)                           │
     │ │           ├── JobHistory.tsx                                          │
     │ │           ├── CreateJobForm.tsx   # + CreateJobForm.test.tsx          │
     │ │           ├── StatusUpdateControl.tsx                                 │
     │ │           ├── FilterSortControls.tsx                                  │
     │ │           ├── jobs.api.ts         # typed endpoint functions          │
     │ │           ├── jobs.types.ts       # mirrors BE schemas                │
     │ │           └── useJobs.ts          # TanStack Query hooks; +           │
     │ useJobs.test.ts                                                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ (logs/ is no longer in the tree — logs live in a named volume           │
     │ backend-logs. See section 7.)                                           │
     │                                                                         │
     │ 7. Docker + Makefile orchestration                                      │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Services                                                                │
     │                                                                         │
     │ services:                                                               │
     │   db:                                                                   │
     │     image: postgres:16-alpine                                           │
     │     environment:                                                        │
     │       POSTGRES_DB: ${POSTGRES_DB}                                       │
     │       POSTGRES_USER: ${POSTGRES_USER}                                   │
     │       POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}                           │
     │     volumes:                                                            │
     │       - db-data:/var/lib/postgresql/data                                │
     │     healthcheck:                                                        │
     │       test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U $${POSTGRES_USER} -d           │
     │ $${POSTGRES_DB}"]                                                       │
     │       interval: 2s                                                      │
     │       timeout: 5s                                                       │
     │       retries: 15                                                       │
     │       start_period: 5s                                                  │
     │                                                                         │
     │   backend:                                                              │
     │     build: ./backend                                                    │
     │     environment:                                                        │
     │       POSTGRES_HOST: db                                                 │
     │       POSTGRES_PORT: 5432                                               │
     │       POSTGRES_DB: ${POSTGRES_DB}                                       │
     │       POSTGRES_USER: ${POSTGRES_USER}                                   │
     │       POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}                           │
     │       DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE: config.settings                           │
     │       DJANGO_SECRET_KEY: ${DJANGO_SECRET_KEY}                           │
     │       DJANGO_DEBUG: ${DJANGO_DEBUG:-False}                              │
     │       ENV: ${ENV:-dev}                                                  │
     │       LOG_LEVEL: ${LOG_LEVEL:-INFO}                                     │
     │       LOG_FORMAT: ${LOG_FORMAT:-text}                                   │
     │       LOG_DIR: /app/logs                                                │
     │       SERVICE_NAME: api                                                 │
     │     volumes:                                                            │
     │       - backend-logs:/app/logs                                          │
     │     depends_on:                                                         │
     │       db:                                                               │
     │         condition: service_healthy                                      │
     │     healthcheck:                                                        │
     │       test: ["CMD", "curl", "-fsS",                                     │
     │ "http://localhost:8000/api/health/"]                                    │
     │       interval: 5s                                                      │
     │       timeout: 5s                                                       │
     │       retries: 20                                                       │
     │       start_period: 30s                                                 │
     │     expose:                                                             │
     │       - "8000"                                                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │   frontend:                                                             │
     │     build: ./frontend                                                   │
     │     depends_on:                                                         │
     │       backend:                                                          │
     │         condition: service_healthy                                      │
     │     healthcheck:                                                        │
     │       test: ["CMD-SHELL", "wget -qO- http://localhost/ >/dev/null ||    │
     │ exit 1"]                                                                │
     │       interval: 5s                                                      │
     │       timeout: 5s                                                       │
     │       retries: 10                                                       │
     │     ports:                                                              │
     │       - "8080:80"                                                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │   vitest:                                                               │
     │     profiles: ["test"]                                                  │
     │     build:                                                              │
     │       context: ./frontend                                               │
     │       target: builder       # multi-stage builder has node + deps +     │
     │ source                                                                  │
     │     command: ["npm", "run", "test:unit"]                                │
     │     environment:                                                        │
     │       CI: "true"                                                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │   playwright:                                                           │
     │     profiles: ["test"]                                                  │
     │     build:                                                              │
     │       context: ./frontend                                               │
     │       dockerfile: Dockerfile.playwright                                 │
     │     depends_on:                                                         │
     │       frontend:                                                         │
     │         condition: service_healthy                                      │
     │     environment:                                                        │
     │       PLAYWRIGHT_TEST_BASE_URL: http://frontend:80                      │
     │                                                                         │
     │ volumes:                                                                │
     │   db-data:                                                              │
     │   backend-logs:                                                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ .env.example provides POSTGRES_DB, POSTGRES_USER, POSTGRES_PASSWORD,    │
     │ DJANGO_SECRET_KEY, DJANGO_DEBUG=False, ENV=dev, LOG_LEVEL=INFO,         │
     │ LOG_FORMAT=text with dev-only sample values; .env is gitignored. Django │
     │  settings build the connection string from these env vars               │
     │ (HOST/PORT/NAME/USER/PASSWORD keys in the DATABASES dict), no inline    │
     │ credentials in any committed file.                                      │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Notes:                                                                  │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Backend Dockerfile runtime stage installs curl so the healthcheck has │
     │  a binary to call. The previous inline-Python healthcheck is fragile    │
     │ under shell-quoting in YAML.                                            │
     │ - Frontend healthcheck uses BusyBox wget (alpine-built-in); curl is not │
     │  in nginx:alpine.                                                       │
     │ - Playwright runs as pwuser (Microsoft's pre-created non-root user in   │
     │ the official image). Set via USER pwuser in Dockerfile.playwright.      │
     │ - Frontend serves the API via nginx in production: nginx proxies /api/* │
     │  to backend:8000 and serves the SPA otherwise. Eliminates CORS,         │
     │ eliminates the dev-vs-prod base-URL split. (In dev, Vite's own          │
     │ server.proxy does the same job.)                                        │
     │ - Logs use a named volume (backend-logs) instead of a host bind-mount.  │
     │ A bind-mount on a fresh clone risks UID mismatch and missing-directory  │
     │ failures during cold-machine make test. Logs can still be inspected via │
     │  docker compose exec backend cat /app/logs/<file> or via stdout (which  │
     │ JSON format preserves).                                                 │
     │ - Playwright + vitest are on a test profile so make up doesn't bring    │
     │ them up.                                                                │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Makefile                                                                │
     │                                                                         │
     │ .PHONY: build up stop clean test                                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ # Bootstrap: create .env from example if missing                        │
     │ .env:                                                                   │
     │  @cp -n .env.example .env                                               │
     │  @echo "Created .env from .env.example"                                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ build: | .env                                                           │
     │  docker compose build                                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ up: | .env build                                                        │
     │  docker compose up -d                                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ stop:                                                                   │
     │  docker compose down                                                    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ # Full reset: containers + volumes + .env                               │
     │ clean:                                                                  │
     │  docker compose down -v --remove-orphans                                │
     │  rm -f .env                                                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ # Cold-machine evaluation entrypoint: builds, runs unit tests + E2E,    │
     │ tears down                                                              │
     │ test: | .env                                                            │
     │  docker compose build                                                   │
     │  docker compose up -d db backend                                        │
     │  docker compose exec -T backend pytest -q                               │
     │  docker compose --profile test run --rm vitest                          │
     │  docker compose --profile test up --abort-on-container-exit             │
     │ --exit-code-from playwright frontend playwright                         │
     │  docker compose --profile test down -v                                  │
     │                                                                         │
     │ make test chains: BE pytest → FE Vitest → Playwright E2E. Any failure   │
     │ exits non-zero. The final down -v ensures the next run starts clean (no │
     │  stale db-data between invocations).                                    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ make test walkthrough on a cold machine                                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Re-stating the gate: only make, docker, docker compose v2, bash,        │
     │ DockerHub. No Node, no Python, no Postgres client.                      │
     │                                                                         │
     │ 1. Bootstrap .env. make test order-only-prerequisite on .env runs cp -n │
     │  .env.example .env if no .env exists. Idempotent.                       │
     │ 2. Build images. db and the Playwright base are pulled from DockerHub / │
     │  mcr; backend, frontend, and vitest are built locally.                  │
     │ 3. Start db + backend. pg_isready healthcheck succeeds in ~5 s. Backend │
     │  entrypoint.sh runs python manage.py migrate then execs uvicorn         │
     │ config.asgi:application --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8000. Backend healthcheck │
     │  (curl /api/health/) flips healthy in ~10–25 s; budget is 30 s + 20     │
     │ retries × 5 s = ~130 s tolerance for slow CI runners.                   │
     │ 4. Run BE pytest. docker compose exec -T backend pytest -q. Blocks      │
     │ until exit. Non-zero exit aborts make test.                             │
     │ 5. Run FE Vitest. docker compose --profile test run --rm vitest runs    │
     │ vitest run in the builder stage of the FE image. --rm cleans the        │
     │ container immediately. Non-zero exit aborts.                            │
     │ 6. Start frontend. Multi-stage build outputs /dist to                   │
     │ nginx:1.27-alpine. nginx config has try_files $uri /index.html plus     │
     │ location /api/ { proxy_pass http://backend:8000; }. Healthcheck via     │
     │ BusyBox wget succeeds within seconds.                                   │
     │ 7. Start playwright. Container image                                    │
     │ (mcr.microsoft.com/playwright:v1.58.2-jammy) has all browsers           │
     │ preinstalled. Playwright globalSetup hits a POST /api/test/reset/       │
     │ endpoint (gated by ENV=test) OR runs manage.py flush --no-input via     │
     │ compose-exec to ensure isolation (decision in open question 12). Tests  │
     │ run; container exits with the test result code.                         │
     │ 8. --abort-on-container-exit --exit-code-from playwright propagates     │
     │ Playwright's exit code as the compose exit code, which becomes make     │
     │ test's exit code.                                                       │
     │ 9. Tear down. docker compose --profile test down -v removes containers, │
     │  network, and the db-data volume (full reset).                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Each step has a single named guarantee; this walkthrough is the         │
     │ cold-machine gate audit.                                                │
     │                                                                         │
     │ 8. Performance plan for millions of jobs                                │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Indexes are listed in section 4. This section covers query strategy,    │
     │ pagination, FE rendering, and verification.                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Latest-status query for the list endpoint                               │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Recommendation: Subquery + OuterRef annotation that returns the most    │
     │ recent JobStatus.status_type per Job. Rejected alternatives (revisited  │
     │ below for the filter case):                                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Prefetch with a sliced queryset — heavy on memory, awkward when       │
     │ paginating.                                                             │
     │ - Denormalized current_status column on Job updated on PATCH — fastest  │
     │ reads but adds write coupling and drift risk.                           │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Async caveat (verified via context7 against Django 5.2 docs): Django    │
     │ does not safely evaluate Subquery/OuterRef-annotated querysets in async │
     │  context. Wrap construction-and-evaluation in sync_to_async inside the  │
     │ service layer:                                                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ from asgiref.sync import sync_to_async                                  │
     │ from django.db.models import Subquery, OuterRef                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ @sync_to_async                                                          │
     │ def list_jobs_with_current_status(*, status: str | None, ordering:      │
     │ str):                                                                   │
     │     latest = JobStatus.objects.filter(job=OuterRef("pk")).order_by("-ti │
     │ mestamp").values("status_type")[:1]                                     │
     │     qs = Job.objects.annotate(current_status=Subquery(latest))          │
     │     if status:                                                          │
     │         qs = qs.filter(current_status=status)                           │
     │     return qs.order_by(ordering)                                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Filter-by-status performance gotcha (THE load-bearing decision)         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ qs.filter(current_status=status) filters on the Subquery annotation.    │
     │ Postgres cannot push this down through an index — every row's latest    │
     │ status is computed before the WHERE applies. At 5M jobs with a          │
     │ 5%-RUNNING distribution, this scans 5M correlated subqueries to return  │
     │ ~250k. Mitigations to evaluate at /spec:design:                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - (a) Partial indexes per status value. CREATE INDEX                    │
     │ idx_jobstatus_running ON jobs_jobstatus(job_id, timestamp DESC) WHERE   │
     │ status_type='RUNNING' (one per status). The list query can then use a   │
     │ LATERAL join or an EXISTS predicate that hits the partial index. Adds 4 │
     │  indexes, kept fresh by Postgres automatically.                         │
     │ - (b) Denormalized Job.current_status. Updated on PATCH inside the same │
     │  atomic block. Fastest filter (WHERE current_status='RUNNING' hits a    │
     │ single index). Adds write-side coupling and one extra column.           │
     │ - (c) Keyset pagination via raw SQL window function. Avoids the         │
     │ annotation entirely; uses DISTINCT ON (job_id) over JobStatus with a    │
     │ LATERAL join. Most flexible, hardest to debug.                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Default until reviewed: option (b) — denormalized current_status on     │
     │ Job. It's the single decision that makes the filter case scale          │
     │ linearly. The history table still preserves full audit trail. Lock the  │
     │ choice via Open Question 10 before phase 2 finishes /spec:design.       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ The plan's previously-stated rejection of denormalization assumed       │
     │ unfiltered list queries; the filter case changes the math.              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Pagination                                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - API: cursor pagination on the list and history endpoints. Cursor      │
     │ encodes (created_at, id) for /api/jobs/, (timestamp, id) for            │
     │ /api/jobs/<id>/statuses/. Stable under concurrent inserts.              │
     │ - FE: paginated UI with Next / Previous controls and a small page-size  │
     │ dropdown. Not virtualization — only limit rows render at a time.        │
     │ Document virtualization as the alternative if scroll UX matters more    │
     │ later.                                                                  │
     │                                                                         │
     │ N+1 elimination                                                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Subquery annotation (or denormalized column, post-decision) removes   │
     │ the per-row latest-status lookup.                                       │
     │ - Detail endpoint is a single Job.objects.aget(pk=id).                  │
     │ - History endpoint is a single filtered queryset with index-only scan   │
     │ via the composite index.                                                │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Query verification at the /spec:design gate                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Seed at minimum 1 million jobs (~3M JobStatus rows) with a realistic    │
     │ status distribution (e.g. 80% COMPLETED, 15% PENDING, 5%                │
     │ RUNNING/FAILED). Run EXPLAIN (ANALYZE, BUFFERS) on:                     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ 1. The unfiltered list (-created_at order).                             │
     │ 2. Each filtered variant (?status=PENDING, etc.).                       │
     │ 3. The detail endpoint.                                                 │
     │ 4. The history endpoint with cursor.                                    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Pass criteria: no sequential scans on jobs_job or jobs_jobstatus;       │
     │ buffer hits <50 for paginated reads. If the chosen filter strategy      │
     │ fails under 1M, revisit options (a)/(b)/(c) above. (EXPLAIN at 10k is   │
     │ insufficient — Postgres flips strategies past ~100k.)                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Connection pooling under uvicorn                                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Default for the take-home: uvicorn --workers 1 in entrypoint.sh. Single │
     │  async worker, single connection pool, simple to reason about and       │
     │ matches Postgres's default max_connections=100. PgBouncer in            │
     │ transaction mode is the production answer; out of scope here. Lock      │
     │ --workers 1 at /spec:design.                                            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ 9. Logging strategy                                                     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Centralized backend logging via Python stdlib logging configured with   │
     │ dictConfig. Two output channels (console + file), two formats (text vs  │
     │ JSON) selected by environment.                                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Configuration                                                           │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Env vars (read from Django settings; defaults defined in                │
     │ config/settings.py):                                                    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ┌──────────────┬──────────────────────────┬──────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┐                                                                    │
     │ │     var      │         default          │            values           │
     │    │                                                                    │
     │ ├──────────────┼──────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┤                                                                    │
     │ │ ENV          │ dev                      │ dev / staging / prod        │
     │    │                                                                    │
     │ ├──────────────┼──────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┤                                                                    │
     │ │ LOG_LEVEL    │ INFO                     │ DEBUG / INFO / WARNING /    │
     │    │                                                                    │
     │ │              │                          │ ERROR / CRITICAL            │
     │    │                                                                    │
     │ ├──────────────┼──────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┤                                                                    │
     │ │ LOG_FORMAT   │ text (dev) / json (prod) │ text / json                 │
     │    │                                                                    │
     │ ├──────────────┼──────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┤                                                                    │
     │ │ LOG_DIR      │ /app/logs in container,  │ absolute or relative path   │
     │    │                                                                    │
     │ │              │ ./logs/ host             │                             │
     │    │                                                                    │
     │ ├──────────────┼──────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┤                                                                    │
     │ │ SERVICE_NAME │ api                      │ identifier in filename and  │
     │    │                                                                    │
     │ │              │                          │ JSON service field          │
     │    │                                                                    │
     │ └──────────────┴──────────────────────────┴──────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┘                                                                    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Default profiles:                                                       │
     │ - ENV=dev → text + color on stderr, text in file, LOG_LEVEL=INFO.       │
     │ - ENV=prod → JSON on stderr, JSON in file, LOG_LEVEL=INFO.              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Filename pattern                                                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ {ENV}-{SERVICE_NAME}-{startup_timestamp}.{log|json}                     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Examples:                                                               │
     │ - dev-api-2026-04-25_143045.log                                         │
     │ - prod-api-2026-04-25_143045.json                                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ startup_timestamp is captured at process start, formatted               │
     │ YYYY-MM-DD_HHMMSS (seconds precision avoids collisions on rapid         │
     │ restarts).                                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Rotation and backups                                                    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ RotatingFileHandler(maxBytes=10 * 1024 * 1024, backupCount=7). Rotated  │
     │ files: <base>.log.1 ... <base>.log.7. Past the 7th, oldest drops off.   │
     │ Size-based rotation keeps the take-home simple; document                │
     │ TimedRotatingFileHandler in CLAUDE.md as the production pattern for     │
     │ daily rotation.                                                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Handlers                                                                │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ┌────────────────────┬───────────────────────┬───────────────────────── │
     │ ──┐                                                                     │
     │ │      handler       │      dev format       │        prod format       │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ ├────────────────────┼───────────────────────┼───────────────────────── │
     │ ──┤                                                                     │
     │ │                    │ colorlog.ColoredForma │                          │
     │ pythonjsonlogger.JsonForm │                                             │
     │ │ Console (stderr)   │ tter — colored level  │ atter — single-line JSON │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ │                    │ + module name         │                          │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ ├────────────────────┼───────────────────────┼───────────────────────── │
     │ ──┤                                                                     │
     │ │ File ({LOG_DIR}/{f │ text formatter        │ JSON formatter           │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ │ ilename})          │                       │                          │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ └────────────────────┴───────────────────────┴───────────────────────── │
     │ ──┘                                                                     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Text formatter: [%(asctime)s] %(levelname)-8s %(name)s — %(message)s,   │
     │ with traceback on exception.                                            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ JSON keys per record:                                                   │
     │ - timestamp (ISO 8601 UTC)                                              │
     │ - level                                                                 │
     │ - logger (module name, e.g. app.jobs.services)                          │
     │ - service, env                                                          │
     │ - message                                                               │
     │ - exc_info when present                                                 │
     │ - structured extra fields via logger.info("...", extra={"job_id":       │
     │ j.id}) flattened into the record                                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Logging conventions in code                                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - backend/config/logging.py — the dictConfig factory called from        │
     │ settings.py.                                                            │
     │ - Module-level logger = logging.getLogger(__name__) in every Python     │
     │ file that emits logs.                                                   │
     │ - Service layer logs:                                                   │
     │   - INFO on every state change (job_created, status_appended,           │
     │ job_deleted).                                                           │
     │   - WARNING on validation failures with only the error type and request │
     │  path, never exc_info=True — the exception chain on a 4xx contains user │
     │  input (e.g. the rejected name value), which we do not want in logs.    │
     │   - ERROR + logger.exception(...) only on uncaught 5xx paths.           │
     │ - API handlers stay quiet (thin); the service layer logs.               │
     │ - Django's django.request logger is wired to the same handlers at       │
     │ WARNING.                                                                │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Dependencies                                                            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Add to pyproject.toml:                                                  │
     │ - colorlog (dev color formatter)                                        │
     │ - python-json-logger (prod JSON formatter)                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Both are tiny, single-purpose, no transitive bloat.                     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ .gitignore                                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ logs/, *.log, *.log.*. (Logs in containers go to the named volume; if a │
     │  host bind-mount is added in dev, this entry catches it.)               │
     │                                                                         │
     │ What not to log                                                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ No request bodies. No DB connection strings. No secret-key prefixes. No │
     │  raw exception messages from Pydantic/Django validation failures (they  │
     │ echo user input).                                                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ 10. CLAUDE.md strategy                                                  │
     │                                                                         │
     │ CLAUDE.md is project memory that future sessions load automatically.    │
     │ Keep it lean (≤200 lines), high-signal.                                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ When created: at the start of phase 2 (immediately after this plan is   │
     │ approved) using the init slash command from the claude-md-management    │
     │ plugin. Initial seed includes only what's known and stable from this    │
     │ plan:                                                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Project purpose (one paragraph).                                      │
     │ - Stack with version pins (Django Ninja 1.6.x, Django 5.2, TanStack     │
     │ Query 5.x, React Router 7.x, Vite 8.x, Tailwind 4.x, Vitest 4.x,        │
     │ Playwright 1.58.2-jammy).                                               │
     │ - Make targets and what each does, including the make test chain (BE    │
     │ pytest → FE Vitest → Playwright).                                       │
     │ - Repo layout pointer (link to README's tree).                          │
     │ - Critical patterns and gotchas:                                        │
     │   - Async ORM rule: no sync ORM in async paths.                         │
     │   - sync_to_async required for: transactions, signals, m2m, complex     │
     │ Subquery/OuterRef annotations.                                          │
     │   - PATCH service must call job.save(update_fields=["updated_at"])      │
     │ after appending JobStatus.                                              │
     │   - Filter-by-status uses denormalized current_status (or whichever     │
     │ option is locked) — the rationale is non-obvious.                       │
     │   - factory_boy is sync — call factories from a sync fixture, then use  │
     │ the returned instances inside async tests.                              │
     │   - thin handlers / fat services boundary.                              │
     │   - Frontend serves /api/* via nginx proxy in compose; Vite proxy in    │
     │ dev. Client always uses relative paths.                                 │
     │   - Logging: env-driven format selection; service layer logs state      │
     │ changes at INFO; never log request bodies, validation exception chains, │
     │  or credentials.                                                        │
     │   - uvicorn --workers 1 for take-home; PgBouncer is the production      │
     │ answer.                                                                 │
     │   - DB reset between E2E runs uses manage.py flush (or test-only        │
     │ endpoint, depending on lock).                                           │
     │ - Test commands (local + container) and where each test layer lives.    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ When updated: after each gate transition, invoke                        │
     │ claude-md-management:revise-claude-md to merge in new learnings. After  │
     │ full implementation, invoke claude-md-management:claude-md-improver for │
     │  a final audit pass.                                                    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Anti-pattern to avoid: don't restate the README. CLAUDE.md is for the   │
     │ non-obvious — invariants and gotchas a fresh session would otherwise    │
     │ miss.                                                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ 11. Open questions for the user                                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ These have defaults baked into the plan; flag any to redirect.          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ 1. Job name mutability — default: immutable post-creation, PATCH only   │
     │ accepts status_type. OK?                                                │
     │ 2. Status set — default: PENDING / RUNNING / COMPLETED / FAILED, no     │
     │ CANCELLED. OK?                                                          │
     │ 3. Frontend host port — default: 8080. OK?                              │
     │ 4. E2E spec layout — default: per-flow files (create.spec.ts,           │
     │ update.spec.ts, delete.spec.ts, filter-sort.spec.ts) with workers: 1.   │
     │ OK?                                                                     │
     │ 5. make test behavior — default: builds, runs BE pytest + FE Vitest +   │
     │ Playwright, exits, tears down. OK?                                      │
     │ 6. CLAUDE.md plugin invocation — default: init at start of phase 2,     │
     │ revise-claude-md after each gate. OK?                                   │
     │ 7. DB-level CHECK constraint on status_type — default: skip; rely on    │
     │ Django TextChoices + Pydantic Enum. OK?                                 │
     │ 8. Data partitioning — default: none at this scope; document as future  │
     │ option in CLAUDE.md. OK?                                                │
     │ 9. Logging defaults — default: text+color in dev, JSON in prod,         │
     │ LOG_LEVEL=INFO, RotatingFileHandler 10 MiB × 7 backups, named volume    │
     │ not bind-mount. OK?                                                     │
     │ 10. Filter-by-status strategy at scale (load-bearing) — default:        │
     │ denormalized current_status column on Job updated on PATCH.             │
     │ Alternatives: per-status partial indexes (no schema change but adds 4   │
     │ indexes) or raw-SQL keyset (most flexible, hardest to debug). Lock at   │
     │ /spec:design. OK with denormalized?                                     │
     │ 11. Connection pooling — default: uvicorn --workers 1. PgBouncer        │
     │ optional. OK?                                                           │
     │ 12. E2E DB reset — default: manage.py flush --no-input via globalSetup  │
     │ hook (no test-only endpoint). Alternative: POST /api/test/reset/ gated  │
     │ by ENV=test. OK with flush?                                             │
     │ 13. FE design exploration scope — default: single                       │
     │ frontend-design:frontend-design pass; skip the playground:playground    │
     │ half (UI is two pages). OK?                                             │
     │ 14. Accessibility smoke in E2E — default: add @axe-core/playwright      │
     │ assertion on the list page (one extra dep, free signal for "Attention   │
     │ to Detail"). OK?                                                        │
     │ 15. Vitest environment — default: happy-dom (faster, sufficient for     │
     │ RTL). OK?                                                               │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Verification                                                            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ After phase 2 + 3 complete, on a fresh clone:                           │
     │                                                                         │
     │ 1. make build succeeds without warnings about missing pins or           │
     │ Dockerfile errors.                                                      │
     │ 2. make up brings the stack up; visiting http://localhost:8080 shows    │
     │ the jobs list page.                                                     │
     │ 3. make test returns exit code 0 on green and non-zero on any failure   │
     │ across BE pytest / FE Vitest / Playwright. Logs from each stage stream  │
     │ to stdout.                                                              │
     │ 4. docker compose exec backend python manage.py shell + EXPLAIN         │
     │ (ANALYZE, BUFFERS) on the list query against a 1M-row seed shows        │
     │ index-only scans, no seq scans.                                         │
     │ 5. Manual API smoke: curl http://localhost:8080/api/jobs/ returns the   │
     │ locked envelope shape; POST returns 201 with Location header; PATCH +   │
     │ DELETE round-trips work.                                                │
     │ 6. Logs verification: docker compose exec backend ls /app/logs/ shows   │
     │ dev-api-*.log; switching LOG_FORMAT=json produces .json files.          │
     │ 7. OpenAPI verification: curl http://localhost:8080/api/openapi.json    │
     │ returns valid JSON; /api/docs/ renders interactive docs.                │
     │ 8. make clean removes containers, network, and the named db-data +      │
     │ backend-logs volumes cleanly.                                           │
